Objective Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.  ## 2. Language The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.  ## 3. Page Design  The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:  ### 1. Dashboard Page - **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard - **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality. - **Elements**:   - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.   - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.   - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.   - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.   - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.   - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.   - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.   - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.  ### 2. Device List Page - **Page Title**: My Devices - **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.   - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.   - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 3. Add Device Page - **Page Title**: Add New Device - **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device. - **Elements**:   - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.   - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.   - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).   - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).   - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 4. Device Control Page - **Page Title**: Device Control - **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings. - **Elements**:   - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.   - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.   - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).   - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.   - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.   - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.  ### 5. Automation Rules Page - **Page Title**: Automation Rules - **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.   - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.   - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.   - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).   - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).   - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.   - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).   - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 6. Energy Report Page - **Page Title**: Energy Report - **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices. - **Elements**:   - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.   - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.   - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.   - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.   - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ### 7. Activity Logs Page - **Page Title**: Activity Logs - **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events. - **Elements**:   - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.   - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.   - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.   - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.   - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.  ## 4. Data Storage  The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:  ### 1. User Data - **File Name**: `users.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|email   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|john@example.com   jane_smith|jane@example.com   ```  ### 2. Device Data - **File Name**: `devices.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|   john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00   jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|   ```  ### 3. Room Data - **File Name**: `rooms.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|room_id|room_name   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Living Room   john_doe|2|Bedroom   john_doe|3|Kitchen   jane_smith|1|Living Room   ```  ### 4. Automation Rules Data - **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true   john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true   jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true   ```  ### 5. Energy Consumption Logs - **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5   john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3   john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6   jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2   ```  ### 6. Activity Logs - **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt` - **Data Format**:   ```   username|timestamp|device_id|action|details   ``` - **Example Data**:   ```   john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights   john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72   jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control   ```  All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

## Section 1: Flask Routes and Data Context

### Overview
This section defines the Flask routes required to implement the SmartHomeManager web app along with the data context variables and types for each route to facilitate correct rendering and logic.

---

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Route:** `/dashboard`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Render main dashboard showing all devices, quick controls, and summaries.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int ŌĆö Total number of devices
  - `rooms`: dict ŌĆö Dictionary with room names and device counts
  - `device_status_summary`: dict ŌĆö Summary info of device statuses
- **Template:** `dashboard.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `dashboard-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Displays total devices and status summary
  - `device-management-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to device list page
  - `add-device-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to add device page
  - `automation-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to automation rules page
  - `energy-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to energy consumption page
  - `room-list` (Div) ŌĆö List all rooms with device counts

---

### 2. Device List Page
- **Route:** `/devices`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** List all devices with their status and quick controls
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict represents a device with attributes (id, name, type, room, status)
- **Template:** `device_list.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-list-container` (Div) ŌĆö Container for device list
  - `devices-table` (Table) ŌĆö Table with device info
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

---

### 3. Add New Device Page
- **Route:** `/device/add`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Form to add a new device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device_types`: list of str ŌĆö List of available device types (Light, Thermostat, Appliance, Camera, etc.)
  - `rooms`: list of str ŌĆö List of available rooms
- **Template:** `add_device.html`
- **Form Elements and IDs:**
  - `add-device-form` (Form)
  - `device-name` (Input) ŌĆö Text field for device name
  - `device-type` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for device type
  - `device-room` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for room
  - `submit-add-device` (Button) ŌĆö Submit new device

- **POST Handling:** Validate input and add device to local storage, then redirect to device list

---

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Route:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Control panel for specific device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict ŌĆö Device details including current status and settings
- **Template:** `device_control.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-name-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device current status
  - `control-panel` (Div) ŌĆö Controls specific to device type
  - `save-settings-button` (Button) ŌĆö Save control settings
  - `back-to-device-list` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to device list

- **POST Handling:** Save updates to device status/settings, update local storage, redirect or refresh

---

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Route:** `/automation`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Manage automation rules
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict contains rule details
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Devices to select for actions
- **Template:** `automation.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `automation-rules-list` (Div) ŌĆö List current automation rules
  - `rule-name` (Input) ŌĆö Input name for new rule
  - `trigger-type` (Select) ŌĆö Trigger type dropdown
  - `trigger-value` (Input) ŌĆö Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Select) ŌĆö Choose device for action
  - `action-type` (Select) ŌĆö Action type (On, Off, Adjust)
  - `action-value` (Input) ŌĆö Value for action
  - `add-rule-button` (Button) ŌĆö Add new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

- **POST Handling:** Add or update automation rules in local storage

---

### 6. Energy Consumption Page
- **Route:** `/energy`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Display energy consumption data and filters
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_data`: list of dicts ŌĆö Consumption records filtered by date or device
  - `filter_date`: date or None ŌĆö Date filter value
- **Template:** `energy.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `energy-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Overall summary
  - `energy-table` (Table) ŌĆö Detailed energy consumption
  - `filter-date-input` (Input) ŌĆö Date input for filtering
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button) ŌĆö Apply date filter
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back

---

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Route:** `/activity`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Show user activity logs with search
- **Context Variables:**
  - `activity_logs`: list of dicts ŌĆö Activity log entries
  - `search_query`: str ŌĆö Search query input
- **Template:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div) ŌĆö Container for logs
  - `search-activity` (Input) ŌĆö Search input
  - `search-button` (Button) ŌĆö Execute search

- **POST Handling:** Search activity logs and filter display

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### General Template Notes:
- Templates located in `templates/{template_name}.html`
- Use the `<h1>` tag for page titles with clear, descriptive text
- Navigation buttons use Flask `url_for()` with route function names
- Consistent naming for element IDs matching design spec


### Dashboard Template (`dashboard.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>SmartHomeManager Dashboard</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Dashboard</h1>
  <div id="dashboard-summary">
    <p>Total Devices: {{ total_devices }}</p>
    <p>Status Summary: {{ device_status_summary }}</p>
  </div>
  <button id="device-management-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('device_list') }}'">Manage Devices</button>
  <button id="add-device-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('add_device') }}'">Add Device</button>
  <button id="automation-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('automation') }}'">Automation</button>
  <button id="energy-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('energy') }}'">Energy Consumption</button>
  <div id="room-list">
    {% for room, count in rooms.items() %}
      <p>{{ room }}: {{ count }} devices</p>
    {% endfor %}
  </div>
</body>
</html>
```

### Device List Template (`device_list.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Device List</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Devices</h1>
  <div id="device-list-container">
    <table id="devices-table">
      <thead>
        <tr><th>Name</th><th>Type</th><th>Room</th><th>Status</th><th>Control</th></tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        {% for device in devices %}
          <tr>
            <td>{{ device.name }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.type }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.room }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.status }}</td>
            <td><button id="control-{{ device.id }}" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('device_control', device_id=device.id) }}'">Control</button></td>
          </tr>
        {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>
</html>
```

## Section 3: Data File Format Specifications

### User Data - `users.txt`
- Pipe-delimited `username|email`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### Device Data - `devices.txt`
- Pipe-delimited with fields:
  - `username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power_state|current_temp|mode|schedule`
- Include various types of smart devices such as Lights, Thermostats, Appliances, Cameras.
- Example lines:
```text
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on||||
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Security Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### Room Data - `rooms.txt`
- Pipe-delimited list of room names
- Example:
```text
Living Room
Bedroom
Kitchen
```

### Automation Rules Data - `automation_rules.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|1|Night Light On|Motion|detected|2|On||true
john_doe|2|Morning Thermostat|Time|06:30|2|Adjust|72|true
```

### Energy Consumption Logs - `energy_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### Activity Logs - `activity_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|timestamp|device_id|action|details`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Triggered manually
jane_smith|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Set temperature to 68
```

---

This design spec covers the required Flask routes, HTML template element IDs, and local pipe-delimited data files structure to fully implement the SmartHomeManager application as requested.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### General Template Notes:
- Templates located in `templates/{template_name}.html`
- Use the `<h1>` tag for page titles with clear, descriptive text
- Navigation buttons use Flask `url_for()` with route function names
- Consistent naming for element IDs matching design spec


### Dashboard Template (`dashboard.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>SmartHomeManager Dashboard</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Dashboard</h1>
  <div id="dashboard-summary">
    <p>Total Devices: {{ total_devices }}</p>
    <p>Status Summary: {{ device_status_summary }}</p>
  </div>
  <button id="device-management-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('device_list') }}'">Manage Devices</button>
  <button id="add-device-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('add_device') }}'">Add Device</button>
  <button id="automation-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('automation') }}'">Automation</button>
  <button id="energy-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('energy') }}'">Energy Consumption</button>
  <div id="room-list">
    {% for room, count in rooms.items() %}
      <p>{{ room }}: {{ count }} devices</p>
    {% endfor %}
  </div>
</body>
</html>
```

## Section 3: Data File Format Specifications

### User Data - `users.txt`
- Pipe-delimited `username|email`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### Device Data - `devices.txt`
- Pipe-delimited with fields:
  - `username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power_state|current_temp|mode|schedule`
- Include various types of smart devices such as Lights, Thermostats, Appliances, Cameras.
- Example lines:
```text
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on||||
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Security Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### Room Data - `rooms.txt`
- Pipe-delimited list of room names
- Example:
```text
Living Room
Bedroom
Kitchen
```

### Automation Rules Data - `automation_rules.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|1|Night Light On|Motion|detected|2|On||true
john_doe|2|Morning Thermostat|Time|06:30|2|Adjust|72|true
```

### Energy Consumption Logs - `energy_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### Activity Logs - `activity_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|timestamp|device_id|action|details`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Triggered manually
jane_smith|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Set temperature to 68
```

---

This design spec covers the required Flask routes, HTML template element IDs, and local pipe-delimited data files structure to fully implement the SmartHomeManager application as requested.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

## Section 1: Flask Routes and Data Context

### Overview
This section defines the Flask routes required to implement the SmartHomeManager web app along with the data context variables and types for each route to facilitate correct rendering and logic.

---

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Route:** `/dashboard`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Render main dashboard showing all devices, quick controls, and summaries.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int ŌĆö Total number of devices
  - `rooms`: dict ŌĆö Dictionary with room names and device counts
  - `device_status_summary`: dict ŌĆö Summary info of device statuses
- **Template:** `dashboard.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `dashboard-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Displays total devices and status summary
  - `device-management-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to device list page
  - `add-device-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to add device page
  - `automation-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to automation rules page
  - `energy-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to energy consumption page
  - `room-list` (Div) ŌĆö List all rooms with device counts

---

### 2. Device List Page
- **Route:** `/devices`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** List all devices with their status and quick controls
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict represents a device with attributes (id, name, type, room, status)
- **Template:** `device_list.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-list-container` (Div) ŌĆö Container for device list
  - `devices-table` (Table) ŌĆö Table with device info
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

---

### 3. Add New Device Page
- **Route:** `/device/add`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Form to add a new device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device_types`: list of str ŌĆö List of available device types (Light, Thermostat, Appliance, Camera, etc.)
  - `rooms`: list of str ŌĆö List of available rooms
- **Template:** `add_device.html`
- **Form Elements and IDs:**
  - `add-device-form` (Form)
  - `device-name` (Input) ŌĆö Text field for device name
  - `device-type` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for device type
  - `device-room` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for room
  - `submit-add-device` (Button) ŌĆö Submit new device

- **POST Handling:** Validate input and add device to local storage, then redirect to device list

---

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Route:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Control panel for specific device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict ŌĆö Device details including current status and settings
- **Template:** `device_control.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-name-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device current status
  - `control-panel` (Div) ŌĆö Controls specific to device type
  - `save-settings-button` (Button) ŌĆö Save control settings
  - `back-to-device-list` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to device list

- **POST Handling:** Save updates to device status/settings, update local storage, redirect or refresh

---

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Route:** `/automation`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Manage automation rules
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict contains rule details
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Devices to select for actions
- **Template:** `automation.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `automation-rules-list` (Div) ŌĆö List current automation rules
  - `rule-name` (Input) ŌĆö Input name for new rule
  - `trigger-type` (Select) ŌĆö Trigger type dropdown
  - `trigger-value` (Input) ŌĆö Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Select) ŌĆö Choose device for action
  - `action-type` (Select) ŌĆö Action type (On, Off, Adjust)
  - `action-value` (Input) ŌĆö Value for action
  - `add-rule-button` (Button) ŌĆö Add new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

- **POST Handling:** Add or update automation rules in local storage

---

### 6. Energy Consumption Page
- **Route:** `/energy`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Display energy consumption data and filters
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_data`: list of dicts ŌĆö Consumption records filtered by date or device
  - `filter_date`: date or None ŌĆö Date filter value
- **Template:** `energy.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `energy-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Overall summary
  - `energy-table` (Table) ŌĆö Detailed energy consumption
  - `filter-date-input` (Input) ŌĆö Date input for filtering
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button) ŌĆö Apply date filter
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back

---

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Route:** `/activity`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Show user activity logs with search
- **Context Variables:**
  - `activity_logs`: list of dicts ŌĆö Activity log entries
  - `search_query`: str ŌĆö Search query input
- **Template:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div) ŌĆö Container for logs
  - `search-activity` (Input) ŌĆö Search input
  - `search-button` (Button) ŌĆö Execute search

- **POST Handling:** Search activity logs and filter display

---

## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications

### General Template Notes:
- Templates located in `templates/{template_name}.html`
- Use the `<h1>` tag for page titles with clear, descriptive text
- Navigation buttons use Flask `url_for()` with route function names
- Consistent naming for element IDs matching design spec


### Dashboard Template (`dashboard.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>SmartHomeManager Dashboard</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Dashboard</h1>
  <div id="dashboard-summary">
    <p>Total Devices: {{ total_devices }}</p>
    <p>Status Summary: {{ device_status_summary }}</p>
  </div>
  <button id="device-management-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('device_list') }}'">Manage Devices</button>
  <button id="add-device-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('add_device') }}'">Add Device</button>
  <button id="automation-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('automation') }}'">Automation</button>
  <button id="energy-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('energy') }}'">Energy Consumption</button>
  <div id="room-list">
    {% for room, count in rooms.items() %}
      <p>{{ room }}: {{ count }} devices</p>
    {% endfor %}
  </div>
</body>
</html>
```

### Device List Template (`device_list.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Device List</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Devices</h1>
  <div id="device-list-container">
    <table id="devices-table">
      <thead>
        <tr><th>Name</th><th>Type</th><th>Room</th><th>Status</th><th>Control</th></tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        {% for device in devices %}
          <tr>
            <td>{{ device.name }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.type }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.room }}</td>
            <td>{{ device.status }}</td>
            <td><button id="control-{{ device.id }}" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('device_control', device_id=device.id) }}'">Control</button></td>
          </tr>
        {% endfor %}
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>
</html>
```

    <input type="text" id="device-name" name="device_name" required>

    <label for="device-type">Device Type:</label>

      {% for type in device_types %}
        <option value="{{ type }}">{{ type }}</option>
      {% endfor %}

      {% endfor %}

  </form>
</body>
</html>
```

</head>
<body>
  <h1>Energy Consumption</h1>
  <div id="energy-summary">
    <!-- Summary statistics here -->
  </div>
  <table id="energy-table">
    <thead>
      <tr><th>Date</th><th>Device</th><th>Consumption (kWh)</th></tr>
    </thead>
    <tbody>
      {% for record in energy_data %}
        <tr>
          <td>{{ record.date }}</td>
          <td>{{ record.device_name }}</td>
          <td>{{ record.consumption }}</td>
        </tr>
      {% endfor %}
    </tbody>
  </table>

  <label for="filter-date-input">Filter by Date:</label>
  <input type="date" id="filter-date-input" name="filter_date" value="{{ filter_date }}">
  <button id="apply-filter-button">Apply Filter</button>
  <button id="back-to-dashboard" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'">Back to Dashboard</button>
</body>
</html>
```

### Activity Logs Template (`activity_logs.html`)
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html>
<head>
  <title>Activity Logs</title>
</head>
<body>
  <h1>Activity Logs</h1>
  <div id="activity-page">
    <input id="search-activity" type="text" name="search_query" placeholder="Search activities" value="{{ search_query or '' }}" />
    <button id="search-button">Search</button>
    <div id="activity-logs-list">
      {% for log in activity_logs %}
        <div class="log-entry">
          <span>{{ log.timestamp }} - {{ log.username }} - {{ log.action }} - {{ log.details }}</span>
        </div>
      {% endfor %}
    </div>
  </div>
</body>
</html>
```

## Section 3: Data File Format Specifications

### User Data - `users.txt`
- Pipe-delimited `username|email`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### Device Data - `devices.txt`
- Pipe-delimited with fields:
  - `username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power_state|current_temp|mode|schedule`
- Include various types of smart devices such as Lights, Thermostats, Appliances, Cameras.
- Example lines:
```text
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on||||
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Security Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### Room Data - `rooms.txt`
- Pipe-delimited list of room names
- Example:
```text
Living Room
Bedroom
Kitchen
```

### Automation Rules Data - `automation_rules.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|1|Night Light On|Motion|detected|2|On||true
john_doe|2|Morning Thermostat|Time|06:30|2|Adjust|72|true
```

### Energy Consumption Logs - `energy_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### Activity Logs - `activity_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|timestamp|device_id|action|details`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Triggered manually
jane_smith|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Set temperature to 68
```

---

This design spec covers the required Flask routes, HTML template element IDs, and local pipe-delimited data files structure to fully implement the SmartHomeManager application as requested.

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

## Section 1: Flask Routes and Data Context

### Overview
This section defines the Flask routes required to implement the SmartHomeManager web app along with the data context variables and types for each route to facilitate correct rendering and logic.

---

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Route:** `/dashboard`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Render main dashboard showing all devices, quick controls, and summaries.
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int ŌĆö Total number of devices
  - `rooms`: dict ŌĆö Dictionary with room names and device counts
  - `device_status_summary`: dict ŌĆö Summary info of device statuses
- **Template:** `dashboard.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `dashboard-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Displays total devices and status summary
  - `device-management-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to device list page
  - `add-device-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to add device page
  - `automation-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to automation rules page
  - `energy-button` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate to energy consumption page
  - `room-list` (Div) ŌĆö List all rooms with device counts

---

### 2. Device List Page
- **Route:** `/devices`  
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** List all devices with their status and quick controls
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict represents a device with attributes (id, name, type, room, status)
- **Template:** `device_list.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-list-container` (Div) ŌĆö Container for device list
  - `devices-table` (Table) ŌĆö Table with device info
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

---

### 3. Add New Device Page
- **Route:** `/device/add`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Form to add a new device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device_types`: list of str ŌĆö List of available device types (Light, Thermostat, Appliance, Camera, etc.)
  - `rooms`: list of str ŌĆö List of available rooms
- **Template:** `add_device.html`
- **Form Elements and IDs:**
  - `add-device-form` (Form)
  - `device-name` (Input) ŌĆö Text field for device name
  - `device-type` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for device type
  - `device-room` (Select) ŌĆö Dropdown for room
  - `submit-add-device` (Button) ŌĆö Submit new device

- **POST Handling:** Validate input and add device to local storage, then redirect to device list

---

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Route:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Control panel for specific device
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict ŌĆö Device details including current status and settings
- **Template:** `device_control.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `device-name-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Span) ŌĆö Displays device current status
  - `control-panel` (Div) ŌĆö Controls specific to device type
  - `save-settings-button` (Button) ŌĆö Save control settings
  - `back-to-device-list` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to device list

- **POST Handling:** Save updates to device status/settings, update local storage, redirect or refresh

---

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Route:** `/automation`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Manage automation rules
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts ŌĆö Each dict contains rule details
  - `devices`: list of dicts ŌĆö Devices to select for actions
- **Template:** `automation.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `automation-rules-list` (Div) ŌĆö List current automation rules
  - `rule-name` (Input) ŌĆö Input name for new rule
  - `trigger-type` (Select) ŌĆö Trigger type dropdown
  - `trigger-value` (Input) ŌĆö Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Select) ŌĆö Choose device for action
  - `action-type` (Select) ŌĆö Action type (On, Off, Adjust)
  - `action-value` (Input) ŌĆö Value for action
  - `add-rule-button` (Button) ŌĆö Add new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back to dashboard

- **POST Handling:** Add or update automation rules in local storage

---

### 6. Energy Consumption Page
- **Route:** `/energy`
- **Methods:** GET
- **Description:** Display energy consumption data and filters
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_data`: list of dicts ŌĆö Consumption records filtered by date or device
  - `filter_date`: date or None ŌĆö Date filter value
- **Template:** `energy.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `energy-summary` (Div) ŌĆö Overall summary
  - `energy-table` (Table) ŌĆö Detailed energy consumption
  - `filter-date-input` (Input) ŌĆö Date input for filtering
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button) ŌĆö Apply date filter
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button) ŌĆö Navigate back

---

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Route:** `/activity`
- **Methods:** GET, POST
- **Description:** Show user activity logs with search
- **Context Variables:**
  - `activity_logs`: list of dicts ŌĆö Activity log entries
  - `search_query`: str ŌĆö Search query input
- **Template:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Main Elements and IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div) ŌĆö Container for logs
  - `search-activity` (Input) ŌĆö Search input
  - `search-button` (Button) ŌĆö Execute search

- **POST Handling:** Search activity logs and filter display

### General Template Notes:
- Templates located in `templates/{template_name}.html`
- Use the `<h1>` tag for page titles with clear, descriptive text
- Navigation buttons use Flask `url_for()` with route function names
- Consistent naming for element IDs matching design spec

  <button id="automation-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('automation') }}'">Automation</button>
  <button id="energy-button" onclick="location.href='{{ url_for('energy') }}'">Energy Consumption</button>
  <div id="room-list">

## Section 3: Data File Format Specifications

### User Data - `users.txt`
- Pipe-delimited `username|email`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```

### Device Data - `devices.txt`
- Pipe-delimited with fields:
  - `username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power_state|current_temp|mode|schedule`
- Include various types of smart devices such as Lights, Thermostats, Appliances, Cameras.
- Example lines:
```text
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on||||
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Security Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

### Room Data - `rooms.txt`
- Pipe-delimited list of room names
- Example:
```text
Living Room
Bedroom
Kitchen
```

### Automation Rules Data - `automation_rules.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|1|Night Light On|Motion|detected|2|On||true
john_doe|2|Morning Thermostat|Time|06:30|2|Adjust|72|true
```

### Energy Consumption Logs - `energy_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

### Activity Logs - `activity_logs.txt`
- Pipe-delimited:
  `username|timestamp|device_id|action|details`
- Example:
```text
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Triggered manually
jane_smith|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Set temperature to 68
```

# Requirements Document for 'SmartHomeManager' Web Application

## 1. Objective
Develop a comprehensive web application named 'SmartHomeManager' using Python, with data managed through local text files. The application enables users to manage smart home devices, control them remotely, set automation rules, and monitor energy consumption. Note that the website should start from the Dashboard page.

## 2. Language
The required development language for the 'SmartHomeManager' application is Python.

## 3. Page Design

The 'SmartHomeManager' web application will consist of the following seven pages:

### 1. Dashboard Page
- **Page Title**: Smart Home Dashboard
- **Overview**: The main hub displaying overview of all devices, quick controls, and navigation to all functionality.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: dashboard-page** - Type: Div - Container for the dashboard page.
  - **ID: device-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total devices, active devices, and offline devices count.
  - **ID: device-list-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device list page.
  - **ID: add-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to add device page.
  - **ID: automation-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to automation rules page.
  - **ID: energy-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to energy report page.
  - **ID: activity-button** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to activity logs page.
  - **ID: room-list** - Type: Div - List of all rooms with device counts, displayed as a dashboard section.

### 2. Device List Page
- **Page Title**: My Devices
- **Overview**: A page displaying all registered smart devices with their status and quick controls.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-list-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device list page.
  - **ID: device-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all devices with name, type, room, status, and actions.
  - **ID: control-device-button-{device_id}** - Type: Button - Button to navigate to device control page (each row has this button).
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 3. Add Device Page
- **Page Title**: Add New Device
- **Overview**: A page for users to register a new smart device.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: add-device-page** - Type: Div - Container for the add device page.
  - **ID: device-name** - Type: Input - Field to input device name.
  - **ID: device-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select device type (Light, Thermostat, Camera, Lock, Sensor, Appliance).
  - **ID: device-room** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select room (Living Room, Bedroom, Kitchen, Bathroom, Garage).
  - **ID: submit-device-button** - Type: Button - Button to submit the new device.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 4. Device Control Page
- **Page Title**: Device Control
- **Overview**: A page for controlling a specific device with detailed settings.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: device-control-page** - Type: Div - Container for the device control page.
  - **ID: device-name-display** - Type: H2 - Display device name.
  - **ID: device-status-display** - Type: Div - Display current device status (Online/Offline).
  - **ID: power-toggle** - Type: Button - Button to toggle device power on/off.
  - **ID: save-settings-button** - Type: Button - Button to save device settings.
  - **ID: back-to-devices** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to device list.

### 5. Automation Rules Page
- **Page Title**: Automation Rules
- **Overview**: A page for creating and managing automation rules for devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: automation-page** - Type: Div - Container for the automation rules page.
  - **ID: rules-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying all automation rules with name, trigger, action, and status.
  - **ID: rule-name** - Type: Input - Field to input rule name.
  - **ID: trigger-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select trigger type (Time, Motion, Temperature).
  - **ID: trigger-value** - Type: Input - Field to input trigger value (e.g., time or threshold).
  - **ID: action-device** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select target device.
  - **ID: action-type** - Type: Dropdown - Dropdown to select action type (Turn On, Turn Off, Set Brightness, Set Temperature).
  - **ID: add-rule-button** - Type: Button - Button to add new automation rule.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 6. Energy Report Page
- **Page Title**: Energy Report
- **Overview**: A page displaying energy consumption data and statistics for all devices.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: energy-page** - Type: Div - Container for the energy report page.
  - **ID: energy-summary** - Type: Div - Summary showing total energy consumption and cost estimate.
  - **ID: energy-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying energy consumption per device with date and kWh.
  - **ID: date-filter** - Type: Input (date) - Field to filter energy data by date.
  - **ID: apply-filter-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply date filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

### 7. Activity Logs Page
- **Page Title**: Activity Logs
- **Overview**: A page displaying all device activity logs and system events.
- **Elements**:
  - **ID: activity-page** - Type: Div - Container for the activity logs page.
  - **ID: activity-table** - Type: Table - Table displaying activity logs with timestamp, device, action, and details.
  - **ID: search-activity** - Type: Input - Field to search activity logs.
  - **ID: apply-search-button** - Type: Button - Button to apply search filter.
  - **ID: back-to-dashboard** - Type: Button - Button to navigate back to dashboard.

## 4. Data Storage

The 'SmartHomeManager' application will store data locally in text files organized in the directory 'data'. The following data formats and examples are defined:

### 1. User Data
- **File Name**: `users.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|email
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|john@example.com
  jane_smith|jane@example.com
  ```

### 2. Device Data
- **File Name**: `devices.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|device_name|device_type|room|brand|model|status|power|brightness|temperature|mode|schedule_time
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
  john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
  jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
  ```

### 3. Room Data
- **File Name**: `rooms.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|room_id|room_name
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Living Room
  john_doe|2|Bedroom
  john_doe|3|Kitchen
  jane_smith|1|Living Room
  ```

### 4. Automation Rules Data
- **File Name**: `automation_rules.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|rule_id|rule_name|trigger_type|trigger_value|action_device_id|action_type|action_value|enabled
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
  john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
  jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
  ```

### 5. Energy Consumption Logs
- **File Name**: `energy_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|device_id|date|consumption_kwh
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
  john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
  john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
  jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
  ```

### 6. Activity Logs
- **File Name**: `activity_logs.txt`
- **Data Format**:
  ```
  username|timestamp|device_id|action|details
  ```
- **Example Data**:
  ```
  john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
  john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
  jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
  ```

All files will be saved in the `data` directory to ensure organization and easy access. The format uses a pipe (`|`) delimiter for better readability and parsing. Different types of data will be isolated to ensure efficient data management and retrieval.

id=\"back-to-dashboard\" onclick=\"location.href='{{ url_for('dashboard') }}'\">Back to Dashboard</button>\n</body>\n</html>\n```\n\n### Add Device Template (`add_device.html`)\n```html\n<!DOCTYPE
