=== LLM_call: BackendDeveloper_SelfReflect ===
INPUT: === Original Task ===
Implement app.py with Flask routes and data handling modules per design_spec.md
=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

=== LLM_call: BackendDeveloper_SelfReflect ===
INPUT: === Original Task ===
Implement app.py with Flask routes and data handling modules per design_spec.md
=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

the spec does not clarify update details so we'll assume add only\n\n        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()\n        trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()\n        trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()\n        action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()\n        action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()\n\n        if not rule_name or not trigger_type or not action_device_id_str or not action_type:\n            # Missing required fields, re-render\n            pass  # Just continue to render with existing\n        else:\n            try:\n                action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)\n            except ValueError:\n                action_device_id = None\n\n            if action_device_id is not None:\n                # New rule_id\n                new_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)\n                new_rule = {\n                    'username': username,\n                    'rule_id': new_id,\n                    'rule_name': rule_name,\n                    'trigger_type': trigger_type,\n                    'trigger_value': trigger_value,\n                    'action_device_id': action_device_id,\n                    'action_type': action_type,\n                    'action_value': '',\n                    'enabled': True\n                }\n                rules.append(new_rule)\n                save_automation_rules(rules)\n                return redirect(url_for('automation'))\n\n    # GET or default render\n    # provide devices with device_id and device_name\n    devices = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices_all]\n\n    return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=devices)\n\n\n# 7. Energy Report Page\n@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])\ndef energy():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n\n    # Enrich energy_records with device_name\n    device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}\n\n    # Optional date filter\n    date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter', None)\n\n    filtered_records = []\n    for r in energy_records:\n        if date_filter and r['date'] != date_filter:\n            continue\n        dev_name = device_name_map.get(r['device_id'], '')\n        rec = {\n            'username': r['username'],\n            'device_id': r['device_id'],\n            'device_name': dev_name,\n            'date': r['date'],\n            'consumption_kwh': r['consumption_kwh'],\n        }\n        filtered_records.append(rec)\n\n    return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)\n\n\n# 8. === design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

Add Device Page\n@app.route('/device/add', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef add_device():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n    rooms = read_rooms(username)\n\n    device_types = sorted(set(d['device_type'] for d in devices))\n    room_names = sorted(set(r['room_name'] for r in rooms))\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        device_name = request.form.get('device_name', '').strip()\n        device_type = request.form.get('device_type', '').strip()\n        room = request.form.get('device_room', '').strip()\n\n        if not device_name or not device_type or not room:\n            # Missing required fields, just re-render GET with lists\n            return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)\n\n        new_device_id = get_next_device_id(devices)\n\n        new_device = {\n            'username': username,\n            'device_id': new_device_id,\n            'device_name': device_name,\n            'device_type': device_type,\n            'room': room,\n            'brand': '',\n            'model': '',\n            'status': 'Offline',\n            'power': 'off',\n            'brightness': '',\n            'temperature': '',\n            'mode': '',\n            'schedule_time': '',\n        }\n\n        devices.append(new_device)\n        save_devices(devices)\n\n        return redirect(url_for('device_list'))\n\n    # GET method\n    return render_template('add_device.html', device_types=device_types, rooms=room_names)\n\n\n# 5. Device Control Page\n@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef device_control(device_id):\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n    device = next((d for d in devices if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username), None)\n    if device is None:\n        return redirect(url_for('device_list'))\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        power = request.form.get('power')\n        brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')\n        temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')\n        mode = request.form.get('mode', '')\n        schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')\n\n        if power in ('on', 'off'):\n            device['power'] = power\n            device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'\n\n        device['brightness'] = brightness\n        device['temperature'] = temperature\n        device['mode'] = mode\n        device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time\n\n        save_devices(devices)\n\n        return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))\n\n    device_context = {\n        'device_id': device['device_id'],\n        'device_name': device['device_name'],\n        'status': device['status'],\n        'power': device['power'],\n        'brightness': device['brightness'],\n        'temperature': device['temperature'],\n        'mode': device['mode'],\n        'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],\n    }\n    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_context)\n\n\n# 6. Automation Rules Page\n@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef automation():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    rules = read_automation_rules(username)\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()\n        trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()\n        trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()\n        action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()\n        action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()\n\n        if rule_name and trigger_type and action_device_id_str.isdigit() and action_type:\n            action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)\n            new_rule_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)\n            new_rule = {\n                'username': username,\n                'rule_id': new_rule_id,\n                'rule_name': rule_name,\n                'trigger_type': trigger_type,\n                'trigger_value': trigger_value,\n                'action_device_id': action_device_id,\n                'action_type': action_type,\n                'action_value': '',  # Empty as per spec\n                'enabled': True\n            }\n            rules.append(new_rule)\n            save_automation_rules(rules)\n            return redirect(url_for('automation'))\n\n    device_select_list = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices]\n    return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=device_select_list)\n\n\n# 7. Energy Report Page\n@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])\ndef energy():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n\n    device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}\n\n    date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter')\n\n    filtered_records = []\n    for record in energy_records:\n        if date_filter and record['date'] != date_filter:\n            continue\n        filtered_records.append({\n            'username': record['username'],\n            'device_id': record['device_id'],\n            'device_name': device_name_map.get(record['device_id'], ''),\n            'date': record['date'],\n            'consumption_kwh': record['consumption_kwh'],\n        })\n\n    return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)\n\n\n# 8. Activity Logs Page\n@app.route('/activity', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef activity_logs():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    logs = read_activity_logs(username)\n\n    search_query = None\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        search_query = request.form.get('search_query', '').strip()\n        if search_query:\n            logs = [log for log in logs if search_query.lower() in log['action'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['details'].lower() or search_query.lower() in log['username'].lower()]\n\n    return render_template('activity_logs.html', logs=logs, search_query=search_query)\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    app.run(debug=True, port=5000)\n"})

=== design_spec.md ===
# SmartHomeManager Design Specification

---

## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification

### 1. Root Route
- **Endpoint URL:** `/`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
- **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to dashboard)
- **Context Variables:** None

### 2. Dashboard Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/dashboard`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `dashboard`
- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `total_devices`: int
  - `active_devices`: int
  - `offline_devices`: int
  - `rooms`: dict[str, int]  # Room names to device counts

### 3. Device List Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/devices`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `device_list`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_list.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `devices`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `device_type`: str
    - `room`: str
    - `status`: str

### 4. Add Device Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/add`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `add_device`
- **Template Rendered:** `add_device.html`
- **Context Variables (GET):**
  - `device_types`: list[str]
  - `rooms`: list[str]
- **POST behaviour:** Process add device form data and redirect to device list.

### 5. Device Control Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/device/<int:device_id>/control`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `device_control`
- **Template Rendered:** `device_control.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `device`: dict with keys:
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `status`: str
    - `power`: str
    - other device settings may be included.
- **POST behaviour:** Save control changes and redirect or reload.

### 6. Automation Rules Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/automation`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `automation`
- **Template Rendered:** `automation.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `automation_rules`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `rule_id`: int
    - `rule_name`: str
    - `trigger_type`: str
    - `trigger_value`: str
    - `action_device_id`: int
    - `action_type`: str
    - `action_value`: str or empty
    - `enabled`: bool
  - `devices`: list of dicts with `device_id` and `device_name`
- **POST behaviour:** Add or update rules.

### 7. Energy Report Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/energy`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET
- **Function Name:** `energy`
- **Template Rendered:** `energy.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `energy_records`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `device_name`: str
    - `date`: str
    - `consumption_kwh`: float
  - `date_filter`: str or None

### 8. Activity Logs Page
- **Endpoint URL:** `/activity`
- **HTTP Methods:** GET, POST
- **Function Name:** `activity_logs`
- **Template Rendered:** `activity_logs.html`
- **Context Variables:**
  - `logs`: list of dicts with keys:
    - `username`: str
    - `timestamp`: str
    - `device_id`: int
    - `action`: str
    - `details`: str
  - `search_query`: str or None

---

## Section 2: HTML Templates Specification

### Template: `dashboard.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/dashboard.html`
- **Page Title:** "Smart Home Dashboard"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `dashboard-page` (Div): Dashboard container
  - `device-summary` (Div): Summary block with total, active, offline counts
  - `device-list-button` (Button): Link to `/devices`
  - `add-device-button` (Button): Link to `/device/add`
  - `automation-button` (Button): Link to `/automation`
  - `energy-button` (Button): Link to `/energy`
  - `activity-button` (Button): Link to `/activity`
  - `room-list` (Div): List rooms with their device count

### Template: `device_list.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_list.html`
- **Page Title:** "My Devices"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-list-page` (Div): Container div
  - `device-table` (Table): Device info table
  - `control-device-button-{device_id}` (Button): For each device, navigates to control page
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`
- **Dynamic ID Pattern:** `control-device-button-{device_id}` where `{device_id}` is replaced with device ID

### Template: `add_device.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/add_device.html`
- **Page Title:** "Add New Device"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `add-device-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name` (Input): Text input for the device name
  - `device-type` (Dropdown): Device type selection
  - `device-room` (Dropdown): Room selection
  - `submit-device-button` (Button): Submit add device form
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `device_control.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/device_control.html`
- **Page Title:** "Device Control"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `device-control-page` (Div): Container
  - `device-name-display` (H2): Displays device name
  - `device-status-display` (Div): Displays current device status
  - `power-toggle` (Button): Toggle device power
  - `save-settings-button` (Button): Save device settings
  - `back-to-devices` (Button): Link to `/devices`

### Template: `automation.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/automation.html`
- **Page Title:** "Automation Rules"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `automation-page` (Div): Container
  - `rules-table` (Table): Automation rules list
  - `rule-name` (Input): Rule name input
  - `trigger-type` (Dropdown): Trigger type selection
  - `trigger-value` (Input): Trigger value input
  - `action-device` (Dropdown): Action target device selection
  - `action-type` (Dropdown): Action type selection
  - `add-rule-button` (Button): Submit new rule
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `energy.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/energy.html`
- **Page Title:** "Energy Report"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `energy-page` (Div): Container
  - `energy-summary` (Div): Energy stats summary
  - `energy-table` (Table): Energy data per device with date and consumption
  - `date-filter` (Input type date): Date filter for energy data
  - `apply-filter-button` (Button): Apply filter button
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

### Template: `activity_logs.html`
- **Filepath:** `templates/activity_logs.html`
- **Page Title:** "Activity Logs"
- **Element IDs:**
  - `activity-page` (Div): Container
  - `activity-table` (Table): Activity logs
  - `search-activity` (Input): Search input field
  - `apply-search-button` (Button): Apply search
  - `back-to-dashboard` (Button): Link to `/dashboard`

---

## Section 3: Data File Schemas

### 1. `data/users.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)  
  2. `email` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|john@example.com
jane_smith|jane@example.com
```
- No header line; strict pipe-delimited fields

---

### 2. `data/devices.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `device_name` (str)
  4. `device_type` (str)
  5. `room` (str)
  6. `brand` (str)
  7. `model` (str)
  8. `status` (str) e.g. Online/Offline
  9. `power` (str) e.g. "on" or "off"
  10. `brightness` (str) or empty
  11. `temperature` (str) or empty
  12. `mode` (str)
  13. `schedule_time` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room Light|Light|Living Room|Philips|Hue|Online|on|75|||Auto|
john_doe|2|Bedroom Thermostat|Thermostat|Bedroom|Nest|Learning|Online|on||72|Auto|22:00
jane_smith|3|Kitchen Camera|Camera|Kitchen|Ring|Indoor|Online|on||||Manual|
```

---

### 3. `data/rooms.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `room_id` (int)
  3. `room_name` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Living Room
john_doe|2|Bedroom
john_doe|3|Kitchen
jane_smith|1|Living Room
```

---

### 4. `data/automation_rules.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `rule_id` (int)
  3. `rule_name` (str)
  4. `trigger_type` (str)
  5. `trigger_value` (str)
  6. `action_device_id` (int)
  7. `action_type` (str)
  8. `action_value` (str) or empty
  9. `enabled` (bool as string "true" or "false")
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|Morning Lights|Time|07:00|1|Turn On||true
john_doe|2|Night Mode|Time|22:00|1|Set Brightness|20|true
jane_smith|1|Motion Alert|Motion|detected|3|Turn On||true
```

---

### 5. `data/energy_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `device_id` (int)
  3. `date` (str in YYYY-MM-DD format)
  4. `consumption_kwh` (float)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|1|2024-11-01|0.5
john_doe|2|2024-11-01|2.3
john_doe|1|2024-11-02|0.6
jane_smith|3|2024-11-01|0.2
```

---

### 6. `data/activity_logs.txt`
- Fields (pipe-delimited):
  1. `username` (str)
  2. `timestamp` (str datetime in "YYYY-MM-DD HH:MM:SS" format)
  3. `device_id` (int)
  4. `action` (str)
  5. `details` (str)
- Example lines:
```
john_doe|2024-11-01 07:00:00|1|Power On|Automation triggered: Morning Lights
john_doe|2024-11-01 08:30:00|2|Settings Changed|Temperature set to 72
jane_smith|2024-11-01 09:15:00|3|Power On|Manual control
```

---

This document fully specifies the Flask routes and function handlers, front-end templates with precise element IDs, and the local file data schemas with examples, enabling frontend and backend teams to develop independently and cohesively.

Device Control\n@app.route('/device/<int:device_id>/control', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef device_control(device_id):\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n    device = next((d for d in devices if d['device_id'] == device_id and d['username'] == username), None)\n    if device is None:\n        return redirect(url_for('device_list'))\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        power = request.form.get('power')\n        brightness = request.form.get('brightness', '')\n        temperature = request.form.get('temperature', '')\n        mode = request.form.get('mode', '')\n        schedule_time = request.form.get('schedule_time', '')\n\n        if power in ('on', 'off'):\n            device['power'] = power\n            device['status'] = 'Online' if power == 'on' else 'Offline'\n\n        device['brightness'] = brightness\n        device['temperature'] = temperature\n        device['mode'] = mode\n        device['schedule_time'] = schedule_time\n\n        save_devices(devices)\n        return redirect(url_for('device_control', device_id=device_id))\n\n    device_ctx = {\n        'device_id': device['device_id'],\n        'device_name': device['device_name'],\n        'status': device['status'],\n        'power': device['power'],\n        'brightness': device['brightness'],\n        'temperature': device['temperature'],\n        'mode': device['mode'],\n        'schedule_time': device['schedule_time'],\n    }\n    return render_template('device_control.html', device=device_ctx)\n\n# 6. Automation Rules\n@app.route('/automation', methods=['GET', 'POST'])\ndef automation():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    rules = read_automation_rules(username)\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n\n    if request.method == 'POST':\n        rule_name = request.form.get('rule_name', '').strip()\n        trigger_type = request.form.get('trigger_type', '').strip()\n        trigger_value = request.form.get('trigger_value', '').strip()\n        action_device_id_str = request.form.get('action_device', '').strip()\n        action_type = request.form.get('action_type', '').strip()\n\n        if rule_name and trigger_type and action_device_id_str.isdigit() and action_type:\n            action_device_id = int(action_device_id_str)\n            new_rule_id = get_next_rule_id(rules)\n            new_rule = {\n                'username': username,\n                'rule_id': new_rule_id,\n                'rule_name': rule_name,\n                'trigger_type': trigger_type,\n                'trigger_value': trigger_value,\n                'action_device_id': action_device_id,\n                'action_type': action_type,\n                'action_value': '',\n                'enabled': True,\n            }\n            rules.append(new_rule)\n            save_automation_rules(rules)\n            return redirect(url_for('automation'))\n\n    devices_select = [{'device_id': d['device_id'], 'device_name': d['device_name']} for d in devices]\n    return render_template('automation.html', automation_rules=rules, devices=devices_select)\n\n# 7. Energy Report\n@app.route('/energy', methods=['GET'])\ndef energy():\n    username = DEFAULT_USERNAME\n    energy_records = read_energy_logs(username)\n    devices = read_devices(username)\n\n    device_name_map = {d['device_id']: d['device_name'] for d in devices}\n\n    date_filter = request.args.get('date_filter')\n\n    filtered_records = []\n    for record in energy_records:\n        if date_filter and record['date'] != date_filter:\n            continue\n        filtered_records.append({\n            'username': record['username'],\n            'device_id': record['device_id'],\n            'device_name': device_name_map.get(record['device_id'], ''),\n            'date': record['date'],\n            'consumption_kwh': record['consumption_kwh'],\n        })\n\n    return render_template('energy.html', energy_records=filtered_records, date_filter=date_filter)\n\n# 8.
